# awesome-python  [![Awesome](https://awesome.re/badge.svg)](https://awesome.re)

with an emphasis on data and machine learning, organised by category üêç  

Interactive version: [www.awesomepython.org](https://www.awesomepython.org/)

Updated 31 Jan 2024

## Machine Learning - Reinforcement
